\subsection{详细描述}
Include file that supports U\+E\+FI.

\hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} include file must contain things defined in the U\+E\+FI 2.\+3 specification. If a code construct is defined in the U\+E\+FI 2.\+3 specification it must be included by this include file.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_aee5e0c5ccb7e884a287da021b444f0c6}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} Type, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_multi_phase_8h_a0e2cdd0290e753cca604d3977cbe8bb9}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} Memory\+Type, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Pages, IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a31bc7e7faeab8d2940ee34f21d41cd04}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+P\+H\+Y\+S\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+SS} $\ast$Memory)}

Allocates memory pages from the system.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Type} & The type of allocation to perform. \\
\hline
{\em Memory\+Type} & The type of memory to allocate. \\
\hline
{\em Pages} & The number of contiguous 4 KB pages to allocate. \\
\hline
{\em Memory} & The pointer to a physical address. On input, the way in which the address is used depends on the value of Type.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The requested pages were allocated. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & 1) Type is not Allocate\+Any\+Pages or Allocate\+Max\+Address or Allocate\+Address. 2) Memory\+Type is in the range 3) Memory is N\+U\+LL. Efi\+Max\+Memory\+Type..0x7\+F\+F\+F\+F\+F\+FF. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & The pages could not be allocated. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & The requested pages could not be found. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}}
\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}{EFI\_CLOSE\_PROTOCOL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Agent\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Controller\+Handle)}

Closes a protocol on a handle that was opened using Open\+Protocol().


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Handle} & The handle for the protocol interface that was previously opened with Open\+Protocol(), and is now being closed. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & The published unique identifier of the protocol. \\
\hline
{\em Agent\+Handle} & The handle of the agent that is closing the protocol interface. \\
\hline
{\em Controller\+Handle} & If the agent that opened a protocol is a driver that follows the U\+E\+FI Driver Model, then this parameter is the controller handle that required the protocol interface.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The protocol instance was closed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & 1) Handle is N\+U\+LL. 2) Agent\+Handle is N\+U\+LL. 3) Controller\+Handle is not N\+U\+LL and Controller\+Handle is not a valid E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE. 4) \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & 1) Handle does not support the protocol specified by \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}. 2) The protocol interface specified by Handle and \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is not currently open by Agent\+Handle and Controller\+Handle. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_a783ca2b09f5bfa720b9dd5e8bb16a557}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_a783ca2b09f5bfa720b9dd5e8bb16a557}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+ER}{EFI\_CONNECT\_CONTROLLER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+ER) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Controller\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$Driver\+Image\+Handle, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___d_e_v_i_c_e___p_a_t_h___p_r_o_t_o_c_o_l}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL} $\ast$Remaining\+Device\+Path, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a112e3146cb38b6ee95e64d85842e380a}{B\+O\+O\+L\+E\+AN} Recursive)}

Connects one or more drivers to a controller.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Controller\+Handle} & The handle of the controller to which driver(s) are to be connected. \\
\hline
{\em Driver\+Image\+Handle} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to an ordered list handles that support the E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL. \\
\hline
{\em Remaining\+Device\+Path} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the device path that specifies a child of the controller specified by Controller\+Handle. \\
\hline
{\em Recursive} & If T\+R\+UE, then Connect\+Controller() is called recursively until the entire tree of controllers below the controller specified by Controller\+Handle have been created. If F\+A\+L\+SE, then the tree of controllers is only expanded one level.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & 1) One or more drivers were connected to Controller\+Handle. 2) No drivers were connected to Controller\+Handle, but Remaining\+Device\+Path is not N\+U\+LL, and it is an End Device Path Node. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Controller\+Handle is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & 1) There are no E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL instances present in the system. 2) No drivers were connected to Controller\+Handle. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+V\+E\+R\+T\+\_\+\+P\+O\+I\+N\+T\+ER}{EFI\_CONVERT\_POINTER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+V\+E\+R\+T\+\_\+\+P\+O\+I\+N\+T\+ER) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Debug\+Disposition, IN O\+UT \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$$\ast$Address)}

Determines the new virtual address that is to be used on subsequent memory accesses.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Debug\+Disposition} & Supplies type information for the pointer being converted. \\
\hline
{\em Address} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to a pointer that is to be fixed to be the value needed for the new virtual address mappings being applied.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The pointer pointed to by Address was modified. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & 1) Address is N\+U\+LL. 2) $\ast$\+Address is N\+U\+LL and Debug\+Disposition does not have the E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+P\+TR bit set. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & The pointer pointed to by Address was not found to be part of the current memory map. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} is normally fatal. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+R\+E\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} Type, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ab998e5f7da4a664eaa86252ab16e459a}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+T\+PL} Notify\+Tpl, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_a7ca9ae93c85ccde1ddaeee99053eb2df}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+FY} Notify\+Function, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Notify\+Context, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a7f3111de303d836d8d3711c39363f81a}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_event}{Event})}

Creates an event.

{\em Type} & The type of event to create and its mode and attributes. \\
\hline
{\em Notify\+Tpl} & The task priority level of event notifications, if needed. \\
\hline
{\em Notify\+Function} & The pointer to the event\textquotesingle{}s notification function, if any. \\
\hline

\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event}} & The pointer to the newly created event if the call succeeds; undefined otherwise.\\

\hline

\hline

Creates an event in a group.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Type} & The type of event to create and its mode and attributes. \\
\hline
{\em Notify\+Tpl} & The task priority level of event notifications,if needed. \\
\hline
{\em Notify\+Function} & The pointer to the event\textquotesingle{}s notification function, if any. \\
\hline
{\em Notify\+Context} & The pointer to the notification function\textquotesingle{}s context; corresponds to parameter \hyperlink{struct_context}{Context} in the notification function. \\
\hline
{\em Event\+Group} & The pointer to the unique identifier of the group to which this event belongs. If this is N\+U\+LL, then the function behaves as if the parameters were passed to Create\+Event. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event}} & The pointer to the newly created event if the call succeeds; undefined otherwise.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The event structure was created. \\
\hline

\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & The event could not be allocated. \\
\hline

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+ER}{EFI\_DISCONNECT\_CONTROLLER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+ER) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Controller\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Driver\+Image\+Handle, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Child\+Handle O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

Disconnects one or more drivers from a controller.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Controller\+Handle} & The handle of the controller from which driver(s) are to be disconnected. \\
\hline
{\em Driver\+Image\+Handle} & The driver to disconnect from Controller\+Handle. If Driver\+Image\+Handle is N\+U\+LL, then all the drivers currently managing Controller\+Handle are disconnected from Controller\+Handle. \\
\hline
{\em Child\+Handle} & The handle of the child to destroy. If Child\+Handle is N\+U\+LL, then all the children of Controller\+Handle are destroyed before the drivers are disconnected from Controller\+Handle.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & 1) One or more drivers were disconnected from the controller. 2) On entry, no drivers are managing Controller\+Handle. 3) Driver\+Image\+Handle is not N\+U\+LL, and on entry Driver\+Image\+Handle is not managing Controller\+Handle. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & 1) Controller\+Handle is N\+U\+LL. 2) Driver\+Image\+Handle is not N\+U\+LL, and it is not a valid E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE. 3) Child\+Handle is not N\+U\+LL, and it is not a valid E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE. 4) Driver\+Image\+Handle does not support the E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+R\+I\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & There are not enough resources available to disconnect any drivers from Controller\+Handle. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & The controller could not be disconnected because of a device error. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+X\+IT}{EFI\_EXIT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+X\+IT) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Image\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US} Exit\+Status, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Exit\+Data\+Size, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a7ae886893bd2a2ae253eb2b021a48724}{C\+H\+A\+R16} $\ast$Exit\+Data O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

Terminates a loaded E\+FI image and returns control to boot services.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Image\+Handle} & Handle that identifies the image. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} parameter is passed to the image on entry. \\
\hline
{\em Exit\+Status} & The image\textquotesingle{}s exit code. \\
\hline
{\em Exit\+Data\+Size} & The size, in bytes, of Exit\+Data. Ignored if Exit\+Status is E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. \\
\hline
{\em Exit\+Data} & The pointer to a data buffer that includes a Null-\/terminated string, optionally followed by additional binary data. The string is a description that the caller may use to further indicate the reason for the image\textquotesingle{}s exit. Exit\+Data is only valid if Exit\+Status is something other than E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS. The Exit\+Data buffer must be allocated by calling Allocate\+Pool().\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The image specified by Image\+Handle was unloaded. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & The image specified by Image\+Handle has been loaded and started with Load\+Image() and Start\+Image(), but the image is not the currently executing image. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_a8d42888e8b015186256055b5f32e0971}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_a8d42888e8b015186256055b5f32e0971}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+X\+I\+T\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+I\+C\+ES}{EFI\_EXIT\_BOOT\_SERVICES}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+X\+I\+T\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+I\+C\+ES) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Image\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Map\+Key)}

Terminates all boot services.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Image\+Handle} & Handle that identifies the exiting image. \\
\hline
{\em Map\+Key} & \hyperlink{struct_key}{Key} to the latest memory map.\\
\hline

{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & Boot services have been terminated. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Map\+Key is incorrect. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+G\+ES) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a31bc7e7faeab8d2940ee34f21d41cd04}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+P\+H\+Y\+S\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+SS} Memory, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Pages)}

Frees memory pages.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Memory} & The base physical address of the pages to be freed. \\
\hline
{\em Pages} & The number of contiguous 4 KB pages to free.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The requested pages were freed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Memory is not a page-\/aligned address or Pages is invalid. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & The requested memory pages were not allocated with Allocate\+Pages(). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+AP}{EFI\_GET\_MEMORY\_MAP}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+AP) (IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Memory\+Map\+Size, IN O\+UT \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___m_e_m_o_r_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+OR} $\ast$Memory\+Map, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Map\+Key, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Descriptor\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} $\ast$Descriptor\+Version)}

Returns the current memory map.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Memory\+Map\+Size} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the size, in bytes, of the Memory\+Map buffer. On input, this is the size of the buffer allocated by the caller. On output, it is the size of the buffer returned by the firmware if the buffer was large enough, or the size of the buffer needed to contain the map if the buffer was too small. \\
\hline
{\em Memory\+Map} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the buffer in which firmware places the current memory map. \\
\hline
{\em Map\+Key} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the location in which firmware returns the key for the current memory map. \\
\hline
{\em Descriptor\+Size} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the location in which firmware returns the size, in bytes, of an individual \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___m_e_m_o_r_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+OR}. \\
\hline
{\em Descriptor\+Version} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the location in which firmware returns the version number associated with the \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___m_e_m_o_r_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+OR}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The memory map was returned in the Memory\+Map buffer. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+S\+M\+A\+LL} & The Memory\+Map buffer was too small. The current buffer size needed to hold the memory map is returned in Memory\+Map\+Size. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & 1) Memory\+Map\+Size is N\+U\+LL. 2) The Memory\+Map buffer is not too small and Memory\+Map is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME}{EFI\_GET\_NEXT\_VARIABLE\_NAME}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME) (IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Variable\+Name\+Size, IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a7ae886893bd2a2ae253eb2b021a48724}{C\+H\+A\+R16} $\ast$Variable\+Name, IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$Vendor\+Guid)}

Enumerates the current variable names.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Variable\+Name\+Size} & The size of the Variable\+Name buffer. \\
\hline
{\em Variable\+Name} & On input, supplies the last Variable\+Name that was returned by Get\+Next\+Variable\+Name(). On output, returns the Nullterminated string of the current variable. \\
\hline
{\em Vendor\+Guid} & On input, supplies the last Vendor\+Guid that was returned by Get\+Next\+Variable\+Name(). On output, returns the Vendor\+Guid of the current variable.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The function completed successfully. \\

\hline

\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & The variable could not be retrieved due to a hardware error. \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+ME) (O\+UT \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___t_i_m_e}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+T\+I\+ME} $\ast$Time, O\+UT \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___t_i_m_e___c_a_p_a_b_i_l_i_t_i_e_s}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+A\+B\+I\+L\+I\+T\+I\+ES} $\ast$Capabilities O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

\hline

\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+LE) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a7ae886893bd2a2ae253eb2b021a48724}{C\+H\+A\+R16} $\ast$Variable\+Name, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$Vendor\+Guid, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} $\ast$Attributes, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Data\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_data}{Data})}

\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline

{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The function completed successfully. \\

\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+S\+M\+A\+LL} & The Data\+Size is too small for the result. \\
\hline

\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Vendor\+Guid is N\+U\+LL. \\

\hline

\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, O\+UT \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$$\ast$Interface)}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+P\+O\+I\+NT}{EFI\_IMAGE\_ENTRY\_POINT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+P\+O\+I\+NT) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Image\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___s_y_s_t_e_m___t_a_b_l_e}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+E\+M\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE} $\ast$System\+Table)}

\hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} is the declaration of an E\+FI image entry point. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} entry point is the same for U\+E\+FI Applications, U\+E\+FI OS Loaders, and U\+E\+FI Drivers including both device drivers and bus drivers.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Image\+Handle} & The firmware allocated handle for the U\+E\+FI image. \\
\hline
{\em System\+Table} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the E\+FI System Table.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The operation completed successfully. \\
\hline
{\em Others} & An unexpected error occurred. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_a7ba493f6b693537a86a17e708cfed4d5}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_a7ba493f6b693537a86a17e708cfed4d5}} 
\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+AD@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+AD}}
\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+AD@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+AD}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+AD}{EFI\_IMAGE\_LOAD}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+AD) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a112e3146cb38b6ee95e64d85842e380a}{B\+O\+O\+L\+E\+AN} Boot\+Policy, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Parent\+Image\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___d_e_v_i_c_e___p_a_t_h___p_r_o_t_o_c_o_l}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL} $\ast$Device\+Path, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Source\+Buffer O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Source\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$Image\+Handle)}

Loads an E\+FI image into memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Boot\+Policy} & If T\+R\+UE, indicates that the request originates from the boot manager, and that the boot manager is attempting to load File\+Path as a boot selection. Ignored if Source\+Buffer is not N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em Parent\+Image\+Handle} & The caller\textquotesingle{}s image handle. \\
\hline
{\em Device\+Path} & The Device\+Handle specific file path from which the image is loaded. \\
\hline
{\em Source\+Buffer} & If not N\+U\+LL, a pointer to the memory location containing a copy of the image to be loaded. \\
\hline
{\em Source\+Size} & The size in bytes of Source\+Buffer. Ignored if Source\+Buffer is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em Image\+Handle} & The pointer to the returned image handle that is created when the image is successfully loaded.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & \hyperlink{class_image}{Image} was loaded into memory correctly. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & Both Source\+Buffer and Device\+Path are N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & One or more parametes are invalid. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & The image type is not supported. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & \hyperlink{class_image}{Image} was not loaded due to insufficient resources. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+A\+D\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & \hyperlink{class_image}{Image} was not loaded because the image format was corrupt or not understood. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & \hyperlink{class_image}{Image} was not loaded because the device returned a read error. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+N\+I\+ED} & \hyperlink{class_image}{Image} was not loaded because the platform policy prohibits the image from being loaded. N\+U\+LL is returned in $\ast$\+Image\+Handle. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+U\+R\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+V\+I\+O\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON} & \hyperlink{class_image}{Image} was loaded and an Image\+Handle was created with a valid \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___l_o_a_d_e_d___i_m_a_g_e___p_r_o_t_o_c_o_l}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+A\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}. However, the current platform policy specifies that the image should not be started. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Image\+Handle, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Exit\+Data\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a7ae886893bd2a2ae253eb2b021a48724}{C\+H\+A\+R16} $\ast$$\ast$Exit\+Data O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

Transfers control to a loaded image\textquotesingle{}s entry point.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Image\+Handle} & Handle of image to be started. \\
\hline
{\em Exit\+Data\+Size} & The pointer to the size, in bytes, of Exit\+Data. \\
\hline
{\em Exit\+Data} & The pointer to a pointer to a data buffer that includes a Null-\/terminated string, optionally followed by additional binary data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Image\+Handle is either an invalid image handle or the image has already been initialized with Start\+Image. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Exit code from image 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+U\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$Guid, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Table)}

Adds, updates, or removes a configuration table entry from the E\+FI System Table.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Guid} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the \hyperlink{interface_g_u_i_d}{G\+U\+ID} for the entry to add, update, or remove. \\
\hline
{\em Table} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the configuration table for the entry to add, update, or remove. May be N\+U\+LL.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The (Guid, Table) pair was added, updated, or removed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & An attempt was made to delete a nonexistent entry. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Guid is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & There is not enough memory available to complete the operation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+C\+ES) (IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$Handle,...)}

Installs one or more protocol interfaces into the boot services environment.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE}{EFI\_INSTALL\_PROTOCOL\_INTERFACE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE) (IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_a623b3b3bad3799f17b8ded654d7235df}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} Interface\+Type, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Interface)}

Installs a protocol interface on a device handle. If the handle does not exist, it is created and added to the list of handles in the system. Install\+Multiple\+Protocol\+Interfaces() performs more error checking than Install\+Protocol\+Interface(), so it is recommended that Install\+Multiple\+Protocol\+Interfaces() be used in place of Install\+Protocol\+Interface()


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Handle} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE on which the interface is to be installed. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & The numeric ID of the protocol interface. \\
\hline
{\em Interface\+Type} & Indicates whether Interface is supplied in native form. \\
\hline
{\em Interface} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the protocol interface.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The protocol interface was installed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & Space for a new handle could not be allocated. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Handle is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Interface\+Type is not E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+A\+T\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is already installed on the handle specified by Handle. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH}{EFI\_LOCATE\_DEVICE\_PATH}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+TH) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, IN O\+UT \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___d_e_v_i_c_e___p_a_t_h___p_r_o_t_o_c_o_l}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL} $\ast$$\ast$Device\+Path, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$Device)}

Locates the handle to a device on the device path that supports the specified protocol.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & Specifies the protocol to search for. \\
\hline
{\em Device\+Path} & On input, a pointer to a pointer to the device path. On output, the device path pointer is modified to point to the remaining part of the device path. \\
\hline
{\em Device} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the returned device handle.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The resulting handle was returned. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & No handles match the search. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Device\+Path is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} handle matched the search and Device is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE}}
\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE}{EFI\_LOCATE\_HANDLE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_abc5a8a9c636f68115cb3956d6e12e27c}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} Search\+Type, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Search\+Key, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Buffer\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$\hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer})}

Returns an array of handles that support a specified protocol.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Search\+Type} & Specifies which \hyperlink{structhandle}{handle(s)} are to be returned. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & Specifies the protocol to search by. \\
\hline
{\em Search\+Key} & Specifies the search key. \\
\hline
{\em Buffer\+Size} & On input, the size in bytes of \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer}. On output, the size in bytes of the array returned in \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer} (if the buffer was large enough) or the size, in bytes, of the buffer needed to obtain the array (if the buffer was not large enough). \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer}} & The buffer in which the array is returned.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The array of handles was returned. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & No handles match the search. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+S\+M\+A\+LL} & The Buffer\+Size is too small for the result. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Search\+Type is not a member of E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Search\+Type is By\+Register\+Notify and Search\+Key is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Search\+Type is By\+Protocol and \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & One or more matches are found and Buffer\+Size is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Buffer\+Size is large enough for the result and \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+ER@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+ER}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+ER}{EFI\_LOCATE\_HANDLE\_BUFFER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+ER) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_abc5a8a9c636f68115cb3956d6e12e27c}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} Search\+Type, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Search\+Key, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$No\+Handles, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} $\ast$$\ast$\hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer})}

Returns an array of handles that support the requested protocol in a buffer allocated from pool.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Search\+Type} & Specifies which \hyperlink{structhandle}{handle(s)} are to be returned. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & Provides the protocol to search by. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} parameter is only valid for a Search\+Type of By\+Protocol. \\
\hline
{\em Search\+Key} & Supplies the search key depending on the Search\+Type. \\
\hline
{\em No\+Handles} & The number of handles returned in \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer}. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer}} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the buffer to return the requested array of handles that support \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The array of handles was returned in \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer}, and the number of handles in \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer} was returned in No\+Handles. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & No handles match the search. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & There is not enough pool memory to store the matching results. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & No\+Handles is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{class_buffer}{Buffer} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}{EFI\_LOCATE\_PROTOCOL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Registration, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL O\+UT \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$$\ast$Interface)}

Returns the first protocol instance that matches the given protocol.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & Provides the protocol to search for. \\
\hline
{\em Registration} & Optional registration key returned from Register\+Protocol\+Notify(). \\
\hline
{\em Interface} & On return, a pointer to the first interface that matches \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} and Registration.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} protocol instance matching \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} was found and returned in Interface. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & No protocol instances were found that match \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} and Registration. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Interface is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL}{EFI\_OPEN\_PROTOCOL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+OL) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, O\+UT \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$$\ast$Interface, O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Agent\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Controller\+Handle, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} Attributes)}

Queries a handle to determine if it supports a specified protocol. If the protocol is supported by the handle, it opens the protocol on behalf of the calling agent.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Handle} & The handle for the protocol interface that is being opened. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & The published unique identifier of the protocol. \\
\hline
{\em Interface} & Supplies the address where a pointer to the corresponding \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} Interface is returned. \\
\hline
{\em Agent\+Handle} & The handle of the agent that is opening the protocol interface specified by \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} and Interface. \\
\hline
{\em Controller\+Handle} & If the agent that is opening a protocol is a driver that follows the U\+E\+FI Driver Model, then this parameter is the controller handle that requires the protocol interface. If the agent does not follow the U\+E\+FI Driver Model, then this parameter is optional and may be N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em Attributes} & The open mode of the protocol interface specified by Handle and \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & An item was added to the open list for the protocol interface, and the protocol interface was returned in Interface. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & Handle does not support \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & One or more parameters are invalid. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+N\+I\+ED} & Required attributes can\textquotesingle{}t be supported in current environment. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+A\+L\+R\+E\+A\+D\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+R\+T\+ED} & Item on the open list already has requierd attributes whose agent handle is the same as Agent\+Handle. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+I\+ON) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, O\+UT \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___o_p_e_n___p_r_o_t_o_c_o_l___i_n_f_o_r_m_a_t_i_o_n___e_n_t_r_y}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+RY} $\ast$$\ast$Entry\+Buffer, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Entry\+Count)}

Retrieves the list of agents that currently have a protocol interface opened.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Handle} & The handle for the protocol interface that is being queried. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & The published unique identifier of the protocol. \\
\hline
{\em Entry\+Buffer} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to a buffer of open protocol information in the form of \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___o_p_e_n___p_r_o_t_o_c_o_l___i_n_f_o_r_m_a_t_i_o_n___e_n_t_r_y}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+RY} structures. \\
\hline
{\em Entry\+Count} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the number of entries in Entry\+Buffer.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The open protocol information was returned in Entry\+Buffer, and the number of entries was returned Entry\+Count. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & There are not enough resources available to allocate Entry\+Buffer. \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+S\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$$\ast$$\ast$Protocol\+Buffer, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Protocol\+Buffer\+Count)}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+A\+B\+I\+L\+I\+T\+I\+ES) (IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___c_a_p_s_u_l_e___h_e_a_d_e_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} $\ast$$\ast$Capsule\+Header\+Array, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Capsule\+Count, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a57be03562867144161c1bfee95ca8f7c}{U\+I\+N\+T64} $\ast$Maximum\+Capsule\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE} $\ast$Reset\+Type)}

Returns if the capsule can be supported via Update\+Capsule().


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Capsule\+Header\+Array} & Virtual pointer to an array of virtual pointers to the capsules being passed into update capsule. \\
\hline
{\em Capsule\+Count} & Number of pointers to \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___c_a_p_s_u_l_e___h_e_a_d_e_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} in Caspule\+Header\+Array. \\
\hline
{\em Maxium\+Capsule\+Size} & On output the maximum size that Update\+Capsule() can support as an argument to Update\+Capsule() via Capsule\+Header\+Array and Scatter\+Gather\+List. \\
\hline
{\em Reset\+Type} & Returns the type of reset required for the capsule update.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & Valid answer returned. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & The capsule type is not supported on this platform, and Maximum\+Capsule\+Size and Reset\+Type are undefined. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Maximum\+Capsule\+Size is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+E\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+FO) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} Attributes, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a57be03562867144161c1bfee95ca8f7c}{U\+I\+N\+T64} $\ast$Maximum\+Variable\+Storage\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a57be03562867144161c1bfee95ca8f7c}{U\+I\+N\+T64} $\ast$Remaining\+Variable\+Storage\+Size, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a57be03562867144161c1bfee95ca8f7c}{U\+I\+N\+T64} $\ast$Maximum\+Variable\+Size)}

Returns information about the E\+FI variables.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Attributes} & Attributes bitmask to specify the type of variables on which to return information. \\
\hline
{\em Maximum\+Variable\+Storage\+Size} & On output the maximum size of the storage space available for the E\+FI variables associated with the attributes specified. \\
\hline
{\em Remaining\+Variable\+Storage\+Size} & Returns the remaining size of the storage space available for the E\+FI variables associated with the attributes specified. \\
\hline
{\em Maximum\+Variable\+Size} & Returns the maximum size of the individual E\+FI variables associated with the attributes specified.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & Valid answer returned. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & An invalid combination of attribute bits was supplied \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & The attribute is not supported on this platform, and the Maximum\+Variable\+Storage\+Size, Remaining\+Variable\+Storage\+Size, Maximum\+Variable\+Size are undefined. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+ER}{EFI\_SET\_TIMER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+ER) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a7f3111de303d836d8d3711c39363f81a}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT} \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event}, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_a813f66495f29a8738fc7be0b60076777}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+AY} Type, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a57be03562867144161c1bfee95ca8f7c}{U\+I\+N\+T64} Trigger\+Time)}

Sets the type of timer and the trigger time for a timer event.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event}} & The timer event that is to be signaled at the specified time. \\
\hline
{\em Type} & The type of time that is specified in Trigger\+Time. \\
\hline
{\em Trigger\+Time} & The number of 100ns units until the timer expires. \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} Trigger\+Time of 0 is legal. If Type is Timer\+Relative and Trigger\+Time is 0, then the timer event will be signaled on the next timer tick. If Type is Timer\+Periodic and Trigger\+Time is 0, then the timer event will be signaled on every timer tick.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The event has been set to be signaled at the requested time. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event} or Type is not valid. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+LE}{EFI\_SET\_VARIABLE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+LE) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a7ae886893bd2a2ae253eb2b021a48724}{C\+H\+A\+R16} $\ast$Variable\+Name, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$Vendor\+Guid, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} Attributes, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Data\+Size, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_data}{Data})}

Sets the value of a variable.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Variable\+Name} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} Null-\/terminated string that is the name of the vendor\textquotesingle{}s variable. Each Variable\+Name is unique for each Vendor\+Guid. Variable\+Name must contain 1 or more characters. If Variable\+Name is an empty string, then E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER is returned. \\
\hline
{\em Vendor\+Guid} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} unique identifier for the vendor. \\
\hline
{\em Attributes} & Attributes bitmask to set for the variable. \\
\hline
{\em Data\+Size} & The size in bytes of the \hyperlink{struct_data}{Data} buffer. \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} size of zero causes the variable to be deleted. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_data}{Data}} & The contents for the variable.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The firmware has successfully stored the variable and its data as defined by the Attributes. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & An invalid combination of attribute bits was supplied, or the Data\+Size exceeds the maximum allowed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Variable\+Name is an empty string. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & Not enough storage is available to hold the variable and its data. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & The variable could not be retrieved due to a hardware error. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+E\+C\+T\+ED} & The variable in question is read-\/only. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+E\+C\+T\+ED} & The variable in question cannot be deleted. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+C\+U\+R\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+V\+I\+O\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON} & The variable could not be written due to E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+V\+A\+R\+I\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+E\+N\+T\+I\+C\+A\+T\+E\+D\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+SS set but the Auth\+Info does N\+OT pass the validation check carried out by the firmware. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & The variable trying to be updated or deleted was not found. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_accb3bf08a31ab1ea83465b40d8469be5}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_accb3bf08a31ab1ea83465b40d8469be5}} 
\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+AP@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+AP}}
\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+AP@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+AP}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+AP}{EFI\_SET\_VIRTUAL\_ADDRESS\_MAP}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+R\+T\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+M\+AP) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Memory\+Map\+Size, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Descriptor\+Size, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ae1e6edbbc26d6fbc71a90190d0266018}{U\+I\+N\+T32} Descriptor\+Version, IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___m_e_m_o_r_y___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+OR} $\ast$Virtual\+Map)}

Changes the runtime addressing mode of E\+FI firmware from physical to virtual.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Memory\+Map\+Size} & The size in bytes of Virtual\+Map. \\
\hline
{\em Descriptor\+Size} & The size in bytes of an entry in the Virtual\+Map. \\
\hline
{\em Descriptor\+Version} & The version of the structure entries in Virtual\+Map. \\
\hline
{\em Virtual\+Map} & An array of memory descriptors which contain new virtual address mapping information for all runtime ranges.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The virtual address map has been applied. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & E\+FI firmware is not at runtime, or the E\+FI firmware is already in virtual address mapped mode. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Descriptor\+Size or Descriptor\+Version is invalid. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+I\+NG} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} virtual address was not supplied for a range in the memory map that requires a mapping. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} virtual address was supplied for an address that is not found in the memory map. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_acf41170aa6f314aaadd5f82a33ab64b7}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_acf41170aa6f314aaadd5f82a33ab64b7}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+W\+A\+K\+E\+U\+P\+\_\+\+T\+I\+ME}{EFI\_SET\_WAKEUP\_TIME}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+W\+A\+K\+E\+U\+P\+\_\+\+T\+I\+ME) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a112e3146cb38b6ee95e64d85842e380a}{B\+O\+O\+L\+E\+AN} Enable, IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___t_i_m_e}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+T\+I\+ME} $\ast$Time O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

Sets the system wakeup alarm clock time.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Enabled} & Enable or disable the wakeup alarm. \\
\hline
{\em Time} & If Enable is T\+R\+UE, the time to set the wakeup alarm for. If Enable is F\+A\+L\+SE, then this parameter is optional, and may be N\+U\+LL.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & If Enable is T\+R\+UE, then the wakeup alarm was enabled. If Enable is F\+A\+L\+SE, then the wakeup alarm was disabled. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} time field is out of range. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & The wakeup time could not be set due to a hardware error. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} wakeup timer is not supported on this platform. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_aa1480f18f35366fab1598f519a4ea2e0}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_aa1480f18f35366fab1598f519a4ea2e0}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+W\+A\+T\+C\+H\+D\+O\+G\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+ER}{EFI\_SET\_WATCHDOG\_TIMER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+W\+A\+T\+C\+H\+D\+O\+G\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+ER) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Timeout, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a57be03562867144161c1bfee95ca8f7c}{U\+I\+N\+T64} Watchdog\+Code, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Data\+Size, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_a7ae886893bd2a2ae253eb2b021a48724}{C\+H\+A\+R16} $\ast$Watchdog\+Data O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

Sets the system\textquotesingle{}s watchdog timer.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Timeout} & The number of seconds to set the watchdog timer to. \\
\hline
{\em Watchdog\+Code} & The numeric code to log on a watchdog timer timeout event. \\
\hline
{\em Data\+Size} & The size, in bytes, of Watchdog\+Data. \\
\hline
{\em Watchdog\+Data} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} data buffer that includes a Null-\/terminated string, optionally followed by additional binary data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The timeout has been set. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & The supplied Watchdog\+Code is invalid. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & The system does not have a watchdog timer. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & The watchdog timer could not be programmed due to a hardware error. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+C\+ES) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle,...)}

Removes one or more protocol interfaces into the boot services environment.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Handle} & The handle to remove the protocol interfaces from. \\
\hline
{\em ...} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} variable argument list containing pairs of protocol G\+U\+I\+Ds and protocol interfaces.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & All the protocol interfaces were removed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & One of the protocol interfaces was not previously installed on Handle. \\

\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_aac9720fc70eb5316876ba3d5f49ca16a}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_aac9720fc70eb5316876ba3d5f49ca16a}}

\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE}{EFI\_UNINSTALL\_PROTOCOL\_INTERFACE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+T\+O\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE) (IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_af943d518ce8a229e7e51ce3fed0e3122}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+LE} Handle, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_ad87614428813f71edb2c2d802e9ce2af}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+G\+U\+ID} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}, IN \hyperlink{interfacevoid}{V\+O\+ID} $\ast$Interface)}

Removes a protocol interface from a device handle. \hyperlink{class_it}{It} is recommended that Uninstall\+Multiple\+Protocol\+Interfaces() be used in place of Uninstall\+Protocol\+Interface().


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Handle} & The handle on which the interface was installed. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol}} & The numeric ID of the interface. \\
\hline
{\em Interface} & \hyperlink{struct_a}{A} pointer to the interface.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The interface was removed. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND} & The interface was not found. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+D\+E\+N\+I\+ED} & The interface was not removed because the interface is still being used by a driver. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Handle is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & \hyperlink{struct_protocol}{Protocol} is N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE}}
\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE}{EFI\_UPDATE\_CAPSULE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE) (IN \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___c_a_p_s_u_l_e___h_e_a_d_e_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} $\ast$$\ast$Capsule\+Header\+Array, IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Capsule\+Count, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a31bc7e7faeab8d2940ee34f21d41cd04}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+P\+H\+Y\+S\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R\+E\+SS} Scatter\+Gather\+List O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL)}

Passes capsules to the firmware with both virtual and physical mapping. Depending on the intended consumption, the firmware may process the capsule immediately. If the payload should persist across a system reset, the reset value returned from E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+Query\+Capsule\+Capabilities must be passed into Reset\+System() and will cause the capsule to be processed by the firmware as part of the reset process.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Capsule\+Header\+Array} & Virtual pointer to an array of virtual pointers to the capsules being passed into update capsule. \\
\hline
{\em Capsule\+Count} & Number of pointers to \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___c_a_p_s_u_l_e___h_e_a_d_e_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+H\+E\+A\+D\+ER} in Caspule\+Header\+Array. \\
\hline
{\em Scatter\+Gather\+List} & Physical pointer to a set of \hyperlink{struct_e_f_i___c_a_p_s_u_l_e___b_l_o_c_k___d_e_s_c_r_i_p_t_o_r}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+OR} that describes the location in physical memory of a set of capsules.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & Valid capsule was passed. If C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+S\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+S\+I\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+R\+O\+S\+S\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+ET is not set, the capsule has been successfully processed by the firmware. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Capsule\+Size is N\+U\+LL, or an incompatible set of flags were set in the capsule header. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & Capsule\+Count is 0. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR} & The capsule update was started, but failed due to a device error. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & The capsule type is not supported on this platform. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+ES} & There were insufficient resources to process the capsule. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_aaba96f688dc14bb2154ce5aceb793493}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_aaba96f688dc14bb2154ce5aceb793493}} 
\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+A\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+A\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT}}
\index{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+A\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT@{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+A\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+A\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT}{EFI\_WAIT\_FOR\_EVENT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a5f446f35c9f907a4f1cf22e794ba338d}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+US}(\hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_aa3998ed6456694d79e9a45f821f379ed}{E\+F\+I\+A\+PI} $\ast$ E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+W\+A\+I\+T\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT) (IN \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} Number\+Of\+Events, IN \hyperlink{_uefi_base_type_8h_a7f3111de303d836d8d3711c39363f81a}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT} $\ast$\hyperlink{struct_event}{Event}, O\+UT \hyperlink{_processor_bind_8h_ac0b1ca9b01db611e0f7f2080a2699135}{U\+I\+N\+TN} $\ast$Index)}

Stops execution until an event is signaled.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em Number\+Of\+Events} & The number of events in the \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event} array. \\
\hline
{\em \hyperlink{struct_event}{Event}} & An array of E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT. \\
\hline
{\em Index} & The pointer to the index of the event which satisfied the wait condition.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS} & The event indicated by Index was signaled. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER} & 1) Number\+Of\+Events is 0. 2) The event indicated by Index is of type E\+V\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+I\+G\+N\+AL. \\
\hline
{\em E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED} & The current T\+PL is not T\+P\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceenum}{enum} \hyperlink{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49}{E\+F\+I\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}

Enumeration of reset types. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{枚举值}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Efi\+Reset\+Cold@{Efi\+Reset\+Cold}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!Efi\+Reset\+Cold@{Efi\+Reset\+Cold}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49a0164249380e07fd1b999f7b611c7fc1b}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49a0164249380e07fd1b999f7b611c7fc1b}} 
Efi\+Reset\+Cold&Used to induce a system-\/wide reset. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} sets all circuitry within the system to its initial state. \hyperlink{namespace_this}{This} type of reset is asynchronous to system operation and operates withgout regard to cycle boundaries. Efi\+Cold\+Reset is tantamount to a system power cycle. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Efi\+Reset\+Warm@{Efi\+Reset\+Warm}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!Efi\+Reset\+Warm@{Efi\+Reset\+Warm}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49add056ce62c5d63bd742b8ef7d4587c85}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49add056ce62c5d63bd742b8ef7d4587c85}} 
Efi\+Reset\+Warm&Used to induce a system-\/wide initialization. The processors are set to their initial state, and pending cycles are not corrupted. If the system does not support this reset type, then an Efi\+Reset\+Cold must be performed. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Efi\+Reset\+Shutdown@{Efi\+Reset\+Shutdown}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!Efi\+Reset\+Shutdown@{Efi\+Reset\+Shutdown}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49ad1b39698e822c87bb227272bb6f791ab}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_aac10574bc0f1e0c24b051d55eb572b49ad1b39698e822c87bb227272bb6f791ab}} 
Efi\+Reset\+Shutdown&Used to induce an entry into a power state equivalent to the A\+C\+PI G2/\+S5 or G3 state. If the system does not support this reset type, then when the system is rebooted, it should exhibit the Efi\+Reset\+Cold attributes. \\
\hline

\hyperlink{class_timer}{Timer} delay types \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{枚举值}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Timer\+Cancel@{Timer\+Cancel}!Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}}\index{Uefi\+Spec.\+h@{Uefi\+Spec.\+h}!Timer\+Cancel@{Timer\+Cancel}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_uefi_spec_8h_a813f66495f29a8738fc7be0b60076777a2c362ea73bc229ab46d950febb9069a5}\label{_uefi_spec_8h_a813f66495f29a8738fc7be0b60076777a2c362ea73bc229ab46d950febb9069a5}}
